    assertions

    Assertions

    Description

    | This Class provides methods which can be used to verify and assert the validations. The methods also allows reporting the PASS/FAIL results into Kibana.

    class Assertions:
    """
    Description:
        |  This Class provides methods which can be used to verify and assert the validations. The methods also allows reporting the PASS/FAIL results into Kibana.

    """

    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = LoggerClass().logger

    class Services:

        request_builder = RequestBuilder()
        json_parser = ResponseParserJSON()
        xml_parser = ResponseParserXML()
        json_parser_util = ParseJsonData()
        xml_parser_util = XMLParser()

        def __init__(self):
            self.assertions = Assertions()
            self.logger = self.assertions.logger

        def verify_is_ok(self, pobj_response, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs):
            """
            Description:
                |  This method can be used to validate if the response status code is 200. When pbool_insert_kibana=True, it inserts the PASS/FAIL status of the step with expected and actual values.

            :param pobj_response:
            :type pobj_response: response object
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: Default is set to True, when True it inserts step PASS/FAIL result in kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param pstr_expected_message: User can use it to overwrite default expected message
            :type pstr_expected_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message: User can use it to overwrite default actual message
            :type pstr_actual_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String

            :return: boolean
             Examples:
                |  verify_is_ok(Response,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Response status code receieved succesfully",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Response status code is not 200")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal

            """
            try:
                int_expected_statuscode = 200
                int_actual_statuscode = self.request_builder.get_response_statuscode(pobj_response)

                bool_result = int_actual_statuscode == int_expected_statuscode
                return bool_result
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_is_valid_http_code(self, pobj_response, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs):
            """
            Description:
                |  (1) When the parameter pint_valid_http_code is passed, this method validates if the response status code is pint_valid_http_code.
                |  (2) When the parameter plist_valid_http_codes is passed, this method validates if the response status code is among the list of status codes in pint_valid_http_code.
                |
                |  When pbool_insert_kibana=True, it inserts the PASS/FAIL status of the step with expected and actual values.

            :param pobj_response:
            :type pobj_response: response object
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: Default is set to True, when True it inserts step PASS/FAIL result in kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param pstr_expected_message: User can use it to overwrite default expected message
            :type pstr_expected_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message: User can use it to overwrite default actual message
            :type pstr_actual_message: kwargs
            :param pint_valid_http_code: Integer
            :type pint_valid_http_code: kwargs
            :param plist_valid_http_codes:
            :type plist_valid_http_codes: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String

            :return: boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_is_valid_http_code(Response,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Valid HTTP code",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Invalid HTTP code")

            .. note::
                |  When both pint_valid_http_code and plist_valid_http_codes are passed to the method, pint_valid_http_code takes the precedence.

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:
                int_valid_http_code = kwargs.get("pint_valid_http_code", 0)
                list_valid_http_codes = kwargs.get("plist_valid_http_codes", [])
                str_error_code = None
                int_actual_statuscode = self.request_builder.get_response_statuscode(pobj_response)

                if int_valid_http_code == 0 and list_valid_http_codes == []:
                    raise Exception(
                        "Error-->Either of the kwargs parameters pint_valid_http_code and plist_valid_http_codes must be passed"
                    )

                if int_valid_http_code != 0:
                    if int_actual_statuscode == int_valid_http_code:
                        bool_result = True
                    else:
                        bool_result = False
                elif list_valid_http_codes != []:
                    if int_actual_statuscode in list_valid_http_codes:
                        bool_result = True
                    else:
                        bool_result = False
                return bool_result

            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_is_invalid_http_code(self, pobj_response, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs):
            """
            Description:
                |  (1) When the parameter pint_invalid_http_code is passed, this method validates if the response status code is not pint_invalid_http_code.
                |  (2) When the parameter plist_invalid_http_codes is passed, this method validates if the response status code is not among the list of status codes in pint_invalid_http_code.
                |
                |  When pbool_insert_kibana=True, it inserts the PASS/FAIL status of the step with expected and actual values.

            :param pobj_response:
            :type pobj_response: response object
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: Default is set to True, when True it inserts step PASS/FAIL result in kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param pstr_expected_message: User can use it to overwrite default expected message
            :type pstr_expected_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message: User can use it to overwrite default actual message
            :type pstr_actual_message: kwargs
            :param pint_invalid_http_code: Integer
            :type pint_invalid_http_code: kwargs
            :param plist_invalid_http_codes:
            :type plist_invalid_http_codes: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String

            :return: boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_is_invalid_http_code(Response,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="invalid HTTP code",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="valid HTTP code")

            .. note::
                |  When both pint_invalid_http_code and plist_invalid_http_codes are passed to the method, pint_invalid_http_code takes the precedence.

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal

            """
            try:
                int_invalid_http_code = kwargs.get("pint_invalid_http_code", 0)
                list_invalid_http_codes = kwargs.get("plist_invalid_http_codes", [])
                str_error_code = None
                int_actual_statuscode = self.request_builder.get_response_statuscode(pobj_response)

                if int_invalid_http_code == 0 and list_invalid_http_codes == []:
                    raise Exception(
                        "Error-->Either of the kwargs parameters pint_invalid_http_code and list_invalid_http_codes must be passed"
                    )

                if int_invalid_http_code != 0:
                    if int_actual_statuscode != int_invalid_http_code:
                        bool_result = True
                    else:
                        bool_result = False
                elif list_invalid_http_codes != []:
                    if int_actual_statuscode not in list_invalid_http_codes:
                        bool_result = True
                    else:
                        bool_result = False
                return bool_result

            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_header_equals(
            self, pobj_response, pdict_expected_header_values, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs
        ):
            """
            Description:
                |  This method validates if the list of headers mentioned in pdict_expected_header_values are present in response headers or not and also checks if the values are as expected.
                |  When pbool_insert_kibana=True, it inserts the PASS/FAIL status of the step with expected and actual values.

            :param pobj_response:
            :type pobj_response: response object
            :param pdict_expected_header_values: Can not be null
            :type pdict_expected_header_values: dictionary
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: Default is set to True, when True it inserts step PASS/FAIL result in kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param pstr_expected_message: User can use it to overwrite default expected message
            :type pstr_expected_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message: User can use it to overwrite default actual message
            :type pstr_actual_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String

            :return: boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_header_equals(Response,header,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Headers are equal",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Headers are not equal")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:
                dict_actual_headers = self.request_builder.get_response_headers(pobj_response)
                list_errors = []

                if len(pdict_expected_header_values) == 0:
                    raise Exception("Error-->pdict_expected_header_values can not be null")

                for k, v in pdict_expected_header_values.items():
                    if k not in dict_actual_headers:
                        list_errors.append(
                            "The header " + k + " is not present in the response headers"
                        )
                    else:
                        if v != dict_actual_headers[k]:
                            list_errors.append(
                                "The header "
                                + k
                                + " has the value "
                                + str(dict_actual_headers[k])
                                + " but the expected value is "
                                + str(v)
                            )

                if len(list_errors) == 0:
                    bool_result = True
                else:
                    bool_result = False
                return bool_result
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_header_exists(
            self, pobj_response, plist_expected_headers, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs
        ):
            """
            Description:
                |  This method validates if the list of headers mentioned in plist_expected_headers are present in response headers or not.
                |  When pbool_insert_kibana=True, it inserts the PASS/FAIL status of the step with expected and actual values.

            :param pobj_response:
            :type pobj_response: response object
            :param plist_expected_headers: Can not be null
            :type plist_expected_headers: list
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: Default is set to True, when True it inserts step PASS/FAIL result in kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param pstr_expected_message: User can use it to overwrite default expected message
            :type pstr_expected_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message: User can use it to overwrite default actual message
            :type pstr_actual_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String

            :return: boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_header_exists(Response,header,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Header exists",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Headers does not exist")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """

            try:
                dict_actual_headers = self.request_builder.get_response_headers(pobj_response)
                list_actual_headers = []
                list_errors = []

                if len(plist_expected_headers) == 0:
                    raise Exception("Error-->plist_expected_headers can not be null")

                for k, v in dict_actual_headers.items():
                    list_actual_headers.append(str(k))

                for i in plist_expected_headers:
                    if i not in list_actual_headers:
                        list_errors.append(i)

                if len(list_errors) == 0:
                    bool_result = True
                else:
                    bool_result = False
                return bool_result
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_header_not_exists(
            self, pobj_response, plist_expected_headers, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs
        ):
            """
            Description:
                |  This method validates if the list of headers mentioned in plist_expected_headers are not present in response headers or not.
                |  When pbool_insert_kibana=True, it inserts the PASS/FAIL status of the step with expected and actual values.

            :param pobj_response:
            :type pobj_response: response object
            :param plist_expected_headers: Can not be null
            :type plist_expected_headers: list
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: Default is set to True, when True it inserts step PASS/FAIL result in kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param pstr_expected_message: User can use it to overwrite default expected message
            :type pstr_expected_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message: User can use it to overwrite default actual message
            :type pstr_actual_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String

            :return: boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_header_not_exists(Response,header,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Header exists",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Headers does not exist")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal

            """
            try:
                dict_actual_headers = self.request_builder.get_response_headers(pobj_response)
                list_actual_headers = []
                list_errors = []

                if len(plist_expected_headers) == 0:
                    raise Exception("Error-->plist_expected_headers can not be null")

                for k, v in dict_actual_headers.items():
                    list_actual_headers.append(str(k))

                for i in plist_expected_headers:
                    if i in list_actual_headers:
                        list_errors.append(i)

                if len(list_errors) == 0:
                    bool_result = True
                else:
                    bool_result = False
                return bool_result

            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_response_sla(
            self,
            pobj_response,
            pint_expected_sla,
            pstr_format="%s.%S",
            pbool_insert_kibana=True,
            **kwargs,
        ):
            """
            Description:
                |  This method validates if the response time is less than or equal to the specified number.
                |  When pbool_insert_kibana=True, it inserts the PASS/FAIL status of the step with expected and actual values.
                |  When
                |  (1) pstr_format == "%s.%f" then response time will be in the form of seconds and microseconds
                |  (2) pstr_format == "%s.%S" then response time will be in the form of seconds and milliseconds
                |  (3) pstr_format == "%M.%s" then response time will be in the form of minutes and seconds

            :param pobj_response:
            :type pobj_response: response object
            :param pint_expected_sla: Can not be null
            :type plist_expected_headers: int
            :param pstr_format: Can not be null, default value is %s.%S and also accepts formats %s.%f, %M.%s
            :type pstr_format: String
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: Default is set to True, when True it inserts step PASS/FAIL result in kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param pstr_expected_message: User can use it to overwrite default expected message
            :type pstr_expected_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message: User can use it to overwrite default actual message
            :type pstr_actual_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String

            :return: boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_response_sla(Response,10,"%s.%f",pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Response time is lesser than expected",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Response time is greater than expected")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:

                if len(pint_expected_sla) == "":
                    raise Exception("Error-->pint_expected_sla can not be null")

                if len(pstr_format) == "":
                    raise Exception("Error-->pstr_format can not be null")

                int_actual_sla = self.request_builder.get_response_time(pobj_response, pstr_format)

                if int_actual_sla <= pint_expected_sla:
                    bool_result = True
                else:
                    bool_result = False
                return bool_result
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def assert_is_ok(self, pobj_response, **kwargs):
            """
            Description:
                |  This method can be used to validate if the response status code is 200. It also inserts the PASS/FAIL status of the step with expected and actual values.

            :param pobj_response:
            :type pobj_response: response object
            :param pstr_expected_message: User can use it to overwrite default expected message
            :type pstr_expected_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message: User can use it to overwrite default actual message
            :type pstr_actual_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String

            :return: boolean
            Examples:
                |  assert_is_ok(Response,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Response status code receieved succesfully",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Response status code is not 200")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:
                assert self.verify_is_ok(pobj_response, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs)
            except AssertionError as ae:
                assertion_err_msg = "Assertion Failed at step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(assertion_err_msg)
                pytest.fail(assertion_err_msg, pytrace=False)
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def assert_is_valid_http_code(self, pobj_response, **kwargs):
            """
            Description:
                |  (1) When the parameter pint_valid_http_code is passed, this method validates if the response status code is pint_valid_http_code.
                |  (2) When the parameter plist_valid_http_codes is passed, this method validates if the response status code is among the list of status codes in pint_valid_http_code.
                |
                |  It also inserts the PASS/FAIL status of the step with expected and actual values.

            :param pobj_response:
            :type pobj_response: response object
            :param pstr_expected_message: User can use it to overwrite default expected message
            :type pstr_expected_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message: User can use it to overwrite default actual message
            :type pstr_actual_message: kwargs
            :param pint_valid_http_code: Integer
            :type pint_valid_http_code: kwargs
            :param plist_valid_http_codes:
            :type plist_valid_http_codes: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String

            :return: boolean
            Examples:
                |  assert_is_valid_http_code(Response,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Valid HTTP code",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Invalid HTTP code")

            .. note::
                |  When both pint_valid_http_code and plist_valid_http_codes are passed to the method, pint_valid_http_code takes the precedence.

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal

            """
            try:
                assert self.verify_is_valid_http_code(
                    pobj_response, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs
                )
            except AssertionError as ae:
                assertion_err_msg = "Assertion Failed at step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(assertion_err_msg)
                pytest.fail(assertion_err_msg, pytrace=False)
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def assert_is_invalid_http_code(self, pobj_response, **kwargs):
            """
            Description:
                |  (1) When the parameter pint_invalid_http_code is passed, this method validates if the response status code is not pint_invalid_http_code.
                |  (2) When the parameter plist_invalid_http_codes is passed, this method validates if the response status code is not among the list of status codes in pint_invalid_http_code.
                |
                |  It also inserts the PASS/FAIL status of the step with expected and actual values.

            :param pobj_response:
            :type pobj_response: response object
            :param pstr_expected_message: User can use it to overwrite default expected message
            :type pstr_expected_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message: User can use it to overwrite default actual message
            :type pstr_actual_message: kwargs
            :param pint_invalid_http_code: Integer
            :type pint_invalid_http_code: kwargs
            :param plist_invalid_http_codes:
            :type plist_invalid_http_codes: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String

            :return: boolean
            Examples:
                |  assert_is_invalid_http_code(Response,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="invalid HTTP code",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="valid HTTP code")

            .. note::
                |  When both pint_invalid_http_code and plist_invalid_http_codes are passed to the method, pint_invalid_http_code takes the precedence.

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal

            """
            try:
                assert self.verify_is_invalid_http_code(
                    pobj_response, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs
                )
            except AssertionError as ae:
                assertion_err_msg = "Assertion Failed at step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(assertion_err_msg)
                pytest.fail(assertion_err_msg, pytrace=False)
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def assert_response_sla(
            self, pobj_response, pint_expected_sla, pstr_format="%s.%S", **kwargs
        ):
            """
            Description:
                |  This method validates if the response time is less than or equal to the specified number.
                |  It also inserts the PASS/FAIL status of the step with expected and actual values.
                |  When
                |  (1) pstr_format == "%s.%f" then response time will be in the form of seconds and microseconds
                |  (2) pstr_format == "%s.%S" then response time will be in the form of seconds and milliseconds
                |  (3) pstr_format == "%M.%s" then response time will be in the form of minutes and seconds

            :param pobj_response:
            :type pobj_response: response object
            :param pint_expected_sla: Can not be null
            :type plist_expected_headers: int
            :param pstr_format: Can not be null, default value is %s.%S and also accepts formats %s.%f, %M.%s
            :type pstr_format: String
            :param pstr_expected_message: User can use it to overwrite default expected message
            :type pstr_expected_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message: User can use it to overwrite default actual message
            :type pstr_actual_message: kwargs
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String

            :return: boolean
            Examples:
                |  assert_response_sla(Response,10,"%s.%f",pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Response time is lesser than expected",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Response time is greater than expected")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:
                assert self.verify_response_sla(
                    pobj_response,
                    pint_expected_sla,
                    pstr_format=pstr_format,
                    pbool_insert_kibana=True,
                    **kwargs,
                )
            except AssertionError as ae:
                assertion_err_msg = "Assertion Failed at step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(assertion_err_msg)
                pytest.fail(assertion_err_msg, pytrace=False)
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_response_contains(self, value: str, response_type: str, **kwargs) -> bool:
            """Verifies if the given value is present within the response
            content.

            This method supports both JSON and XML response types and offers flexibility in extracting values using various methods provided by `ParseJsonData` and `XMLParser`.

            Args:
                value: The value to search for within the response content.
                response_type: The type of response data ("JSON" or "XML").
                **kwargs: Additional keyword arguments to be passed to the respective parser methods (e.g., `json`, `key`, `nested`, `xml`, `node`, `node_xpath`, `ancestor`, `child`).

            Returns:
                True if the value is found within the response content, False otherwise.

            Raises:
                ValueError: If the response_type is invalid or if required kwargs are missing.

            Examples:
                |  verify_response_contains("Value","Json",json=Json_data,pstr_key="key name",pbool_nested=True,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Response contains given value",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Response doesn't contain given value")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:
                bool_result = False
                if response_type.upper() not in ("JSON", "XML"):
                    raise ValueError("Invalid response_type. Please specify 'JSON' or 'XML'.")

                if response_type.upper() == "JSON":
                    if "json" not in kwargs:
                        raise ValueError("Missing required kwarg 'json' for JSON response type.")
                    result = self.json_parser_util.get_json_result(**kwargs)
                elif response_type.upper() == "XML":
                    if "xml" not in kwargs:
                        raise ValueError("Missing required kwarg 'xml' for XML response type.")
                    result = self.xml_parser_util.get_xml_result(**kwargs)
                else:
                    raise ValueError("Invalid response type. Please specify 'JSON' or 'XML'.")

                if result is not None:
                    if isinstance(result, str):
                        bool_result = value in result
                    elif isinstance(result, list):
                        bool_result = any(value in str(item) for item in result)

                self.logger.info("Result is::" + str(bool_result))
                return bool_result
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_response_not_contains(
            self, pstr_value, pstr_response_type, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs
        ):
            """
            Description:
                |  This method checks the given value is partially present in the response,this returns True is given string is not present and execution wont be stopped if this method returns false

            :param pstr_value: pstr_value is the value which should be checked which is in response
            :type pstr_value: String
            :param pstr_response_type: pstr_response_type is the response type(XML or JSON)
            :type pstr_response_type: String
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: pbool_insert_kibana is the boolean value if this is set to True steps will be inserted to kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param json: json is the kwarg parameter ,it accepts string or json data
            :type json: String
            :param pstr_key: pstr_key is the kwarg parameter ,it is the key name of which the value should be fetched
            :type pstr_key: String
            :param pbool_nested: pbool_nested is the the kwarg parameter ,if this is set to true values will be returned in a list otherwise first value will be returned
            :type pbool_nested: Boolean
            :param pstr_keypath: pstr_key is the the kwarg parameter and it is the key path name of which the value should be fetched
            :type pstr_keypath: String
            :param pstr_keypath_type: pstr_keypath_type the kwarg parameter and it is the  key path type i.e.absolute or relative
            :type pstr_keypath_type: String
            :param pstr_key_input: pstr_key_input  is the the kwarg parameter and it is key value  which is presented in key path
            :type pstr_key_input: String
            :param pstr_expected_message: pstr_expected_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the expected value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_expected_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message: pstr_actual_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the actual value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_actual_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String
            :param pobj_api_response: API Response Object
            :type pobj_api_response: Response

            :return: Boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_response_not_contains("Vaue","Json",json=Json_data,pstr_key="key name",pbool_nested=True,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Response contains given value",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Response doesn't contain given value")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:
                bool_result = False
                str_result = None
                if (
                    pstr_response_type == "Json"
                    or pstr_response_type == "JSON"
                    or pstr_response_type == "json"
                ):
                    str_result = self.json_parser_util.get_json_result(**kwargs)
                elif (
                    pstr_response_type == "XML"
                    or pstr_response_type == "xml"
                    or pstr_response_type == "Xml"
                ):
                    str_result = self.xml_parser_util.get_xml_result(**kwargs)
                else:
                    raise Exception("No Response type given")

                if str_result != None:
                    if type(str_result) == str:
                        bool_result = str_result.__contains__(pstr_value)
                    if type(str_result) == list:
                        final_list = []
                        for list_values in str_result:
                            if type(list_values) != list:
                                final_list.append(list_values)
                            else:
                                for nested_list_values in list_values:
                                    final_list.append(nested_list_values)
                        for final_values in final_list:
                            if (str(final_values)).__contains__(pstr_value):
                                bool_result = True
                                break
                            else:
                                bool_result = False
                    bool_result = not bool_result
                return bool_result
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_value_exists(
            self, pstr_value, pstr_response_type, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs
        ):
            """
            Description:
                |  This method checks the given value is present in the response,this returns True is given value is present and execution wont be stopped if this method returns false

            :param pstr_value: pstr_value is the value which should be checked which is in response
            :type pstr_value: String
            :param pstr_response_type: pstr_response_type is the response type(XML or JSON)
            :type pstr_response_type: String
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: pbool_insert_kibana is the boolean value if this is set to True steps will be inserted to kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param json: json is the kwarg parameter ,it accepts string or json data
            :type json: String
            :param pstr_key: pstr_key is the kwarg parameter ,it is the key name of which the value should be fetched
            :type pstr_key: String
            :param pbool_nested: pbool_nested is the the kwarg parameter ,if this is set to true values will be returned in a list otherwise first value will be returned
            :type pbool_nested: Boolean
            :param pstr_keypath: pstr_key is the the kwarg parameter and it is the key path name of which the value should be fetched
            :type pstr_keypath: String
            :param pstr_keypath_type: pstr_keypath_type the kwarg parameter and it is the  key path type i.e.absolute or relative
            :type pstr_keypath_type: String

            :param pstr_actual_message: pstr_actual_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the actual value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana

            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String
            :param pobj_api_response: API Response Object
            :type pobj_api_response: Response

            :return: Boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_value_exists("Vaue","Json",json=Json_data,pstr_key="key name",pbool_nested=True,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Response contains given value",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Response doesn't contain given value")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:
                bool_result = False
                str_result = None
                if (
                    pstr_response_type == "Json"
                    or pstr_response_type == "JSON"
                    or pstr_response_type == "json"
                ):
                    str_result = self.json_parser_util.get_json_result(**kwargs)
                elif (
                    pstr_response_type == "XML"
                    or pstr_response_type == "xml"
                    or pstr_response_type == "Xml"
                ):
                    str_result = self.xml_parser_util.get_xml_result(**kwargs)
                else:
                    raise Exception("No Response type given")

                if str_result != None:
                    if type(str_result) == str:
                        bool_result = str_result == (pstr_value)
                    if type(str_result) == list:
                        final_list = []
                        for list_values in str_result:
                            if type(list_values) != list:
                                final_list.append(list_values)
                            else:
                                for nested_list_values in list_values:
                                    final_list.append(nested_list_values)
                        for final_values in final_list:
                            if (str(final_values)) == (pstr_value):
                                bool_result = True
                                break
                            else:
                                bool_result = False
                return bool_result
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_value_not_exists(
            self, pstr_value, pstr_response_type, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs
        ):
            """
            Description:
                |  This method checks the unavailability of given value in the response,this returns True is given value is not present and execution wont be stopped if this method returns false

            :param pstr_value: pstr_value is the value which should be checked which is in response
            :type pstr_value: String
            :param pstr_response_type: pstr_response_type is the response type(XML or JSON)
            :type pstr_response_type: String
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: pbool_insert_kibana is the boolean value if this is set to True steps will be inserted to kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param json: json is the kwarg parameter ,it accepts string or json data
            :type json: String
            :param pstr_key: pstr_key is the kwarg parameter ,it is the key name of which the value should be fetched
            :type pstr_key: String
            :param pbool_nested: pbool_nested is the the kwarg parameter ,if this is set to true values will be returned in a list otherwise first value will be returned
            :type pbool_nested: Boolean
            :param pstr_keypath: pstr_key is the the kwarg parameter and it is the key path name of which the value should be fetched
            :type pstr_keypath: String
            :param pstr_keypath_type: pstr_keypath_type the kwarg parameter and it is the  key path type i.e.absolute or relative
            :type pstr_keypath_type: String
            :param pstr_key_input: pstr_key_input  is the the kwarg parameter and it is key value  which is presented in key path
            :type pstr_key_input: String
            :param pstr_expected_message: pstr_expected_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the expected value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_expected_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message: pstr_actual_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the actual value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_actual_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String
            :param pobj_api_response: API Response Object
            :type pobj_api_response: Response

            :return: Boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_value_not_exists("Vaue","Json",json=Json_data,pstr_key="key name",pbool_nested=True,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Response contains given value",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Response doesn't contain given value")
                |  verify_value_not_exists("Regular","Xml",xml=xml_string,pstr_ancestor="item",pstr_child="batter")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:
                bool_result = False
                str_result = None
                if (
                    pstr_response_type == "Json"
                    or pstr_response_type == "JSON"
                    or pstr_response_type == "json"
                ):
                    str_result = self.json_parser_util.get_json_result(**kwargs)
                elif (
                    pstr_response_type == "XML"
                    or pstr_response_type == "xml"
                    or pstr_response_type == "Xml"
                ):
                    str_result = self.xml_parser_util.get_xml_result(**kwargs)
                else:
                    raise Exception("No Response type given")

                if str_result != None:
                    if type(str_result) == str:
                        bool_result = str_result == (pstr_value)
                    if type(str_result) == list:
                        final_list = []
                        for list_values in str_result:
                            if type(list_values) != list:
                                final_list.append(list_values)
                            else:
                                for nested_list_values in list_values:
                                    final_list.append(nested_list_values)
                        for final_values in final_list:
                            if (str(final_values)) == (pstr_value):
                                bool_result = True
                                break
                            else:
                                bool_result = False
                bool_result = not bool_result
                return bool_result
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_content_matches(
            self, pstr_expected_content, pstr_actual_content, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs
        ):
            """
            Description:
                |  this method checks the content  of given two josn or xml data in the form of string,returns true if they are equal and execution wont be stopped if this method returns false

            :param pstr_expected_content: pstr_expected_content is value of an expected string
            :type pstr_expected_content: String
            :param pstr_actual_content: pstr_actual_content is value of an actual string
            :type pstr_actual_content: String
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: pbool_insert_kibana is the boolean value if this is set to True steps will be inserted to kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param pstr_expected_message: pstr_expected_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the expected value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_expected_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message: pstr_actual_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the actual value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_actual_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String
            :param pobj_api_response: API Response Object
            :type pobj_api_response: Response

            :return: Boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_content_matches(str1,str2,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Both are equal",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Both are not equal")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            bool_result = pstr_expected_content == pstr_actual_content
            try:
                bool_result = pstr_expected_content == pstr_actual_content
                return bool_result
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_key_count_matches(self, pstr_response_type, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs):
            """
            Description:
                |  this method checks the given key occurance ,given key count are equal or not and execution wont be stopped if this method returns false

            :param pstr_response_type: pstr_response_type is the response type(XML or JSON)
            :type pstr_response_type: String
            :param pdict_json: pdict_json is the json data
            :type pdict_json: String or json
            :param pstr_key: pstr_key is the key of which the occurance will be returned
            :type pstr_key: String
            :param pint_key_count: pint_key_count is the expected key occurance
            :type pint_key_count: int
            :param pstr_xml: pstr_xml is the xml data
            :type pstr_xml: String or xml
            :param pstr_nodepath: pstr_nodepath is the key xpath of which the occurance will be returned
            :type pstr_nodepath: String
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: pbool_insert_kibana is the boolean value if this is set to True steps will be inserted to kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param pstr_expected_message: pstr_expected_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the expected value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_expected_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message: pstr_actual_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the actual value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_actual_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String
            :param pobj_api_response: API Response Object
            :type pobj_api_response: Response

            :return: Boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_key_count_matches("xml",pstr_xml=xml_string,pstr_nodepath="//batter",pint_key_count=3,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Key count matches",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Key count does not match")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:
                int_result = 0
                pint_key_count = 0
                if (
                    pstr_response_type == "Json"
                    or pstr_response_type == "JSON"
                    or pstr_response_type == "json"
                ):
                    pdict_json = kwargs.get("pdict_json")
                    pstr_key = kwargs.get("pstr_key")
                    pint_key_count = kwargs.get("pint_key_count")
                    int_result = self.json_parser.get_occurrence_of_key(pdict_json, pstr_key)
                elif (
                    pstr_response_type == "XML"
                    or pstr_response_type == "xml"
                    or pstr_response_type == "Xml"
                ):
                    pstr_xml = kwargs.get("pstr_xml")
                    pstr_nodepath = kwargs.get("pstr_nodepath")
                    pint_key_count = kwargs.get("pint_key_count")
                    int_result = self.xml_parser.get_element_count(pstr_xml, pstr_nodepath)
                else:
                    raise Exception("No Response type given")
                self.logger.info("Key Occurance::" + str(int_result))
                bool_result = int_result == pint_key_count
                return bool_result
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_key_available(self, pstr_response_type, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs):
            """
            Description:
                |  this method checks the given key occurance ,given key count are equal or not and execution wont be stopped if this method returns false

            :param pstr_response_type: pstr_response_type is the response type(XML or JSON)
            :type pstr_response_type: String
            :param pdict_json: pdict_json is the json data
            :type pdict_json: String or json
            :param pstr_key: pstr_key is the key of which the existance be returned
            :type pstr_key: String
            :param pstr_xml: pstr_xml is the xml data
            :type pstr_xml: String or xml
            :param pstr_nodepath: pstr_nodepath is the key xpath of which the existance will be returned
            :type pstr_nodepath: String
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: pbool_insert_kibana is the boolean value if this is set to True steps will be inserted to kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param pstr_expected_message: pstr_expected_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the expected value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_expected_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message: pstr_actual_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the actual value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_actual_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String
            :param pobj_api_response: API Response Object
            :type pobj_api_response: Response

            :return: Boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_key_available("Xml",pstr_xml=xml_string,pstr_nodepath="topping",pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Key is available",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Key is not available")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:
                if (
                    pstr_response_type == "Json"
                    or pstr_response_type == "JSON"
                    or pstr_response_type == "json"
                ):
                    pdict_json = kwargs.get("pdict_json")
                    pstr_key = kwargs.get("pstr_key")
                    bool_result = self.json_parser.key_exists(pdict_json, pstr_key)
                elif (
                    pstr_response_type == "XML"
                    or pstr_response_type == "xml"
                    or pstr_response_type == "Xml"
                ):
                    pstr_xml = kwargs.get("pstr_xml")
                    pstr_nodepath = kwargs.get("pstr_nodepath")
                    bool_result = self.xml_parser.element_should_exist(pstr_xml, pstr_nodepath)
                else:
                    raise Exception("No Response type given")
                return bool_result

            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def verify_value_matches_regex(
            self, pstr_regex, pstr_value, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs
        ):
            """
            Description:
                |  this method checks the given string is in thr form of given regular expression and execution wont be stopped if this method returns false

            :param pstr_regex: pstr_regex is the regular expression
            :type pstr_regex: String
            :param pstr_value: pstr_value is the value of which the regular expression form should be checked
            :type pstr_value: String
            :param pbool_insert_kibana: pbool_insert_kibana is the boolean value if this is set to True steps will be inserted to kibana
            :type pbool_insert_kibana: boolean
            :param pstr_expected_message: pstr_expected_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the expected value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_expected_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message: pstr_actual_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the actual value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_actual_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String
            :param pobj_api_response: API Response Object
            :type pobj_api_response: Response

            :return: Boolean
            Examples:
                |  verify_value_matches_regex("Va*","Value",pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Given string is in the form of regex",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Given string is not in the form of regex")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:
                bool_result = False
                match_found = re.search(pstr_regex, pstr_value)
                if match_found is not None:
                    bool_result = True
                    match_found = match_found.group()
                    self.logger.debug(match_found)
                else:
                    bool_result = False
                return bool_result
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)

        def assert_response_contains(self, pstr_value, pstr_response_type, **kwargs):
            """
            Description:
                |  This method checks the given value is partially present in the response and execution will be stopped if this method returns false

            :param pstr_value: pstr_value is the value which should be checked which is in response
            :type pstr_value: String
            :param pstr_response_type: pstr_response_type is the response type(XML or JSON)
            :type pstr_response_type: String
            :param json: json is the kwarg parameter ,it accepts string or json data
            :type json: String
            :param pstr_key: pstr_key is the kwarg parameter ,it is the key name of which the value should be fetched
            :type pstr_key: String
            :param pbool_nested: pbool_nested is the the kwarg parameter ,if this is set to true values will be returned in a list otherwise first value will be returned
            :type pbool_nested: Boolean
            :param pstr_keypath: pstr_key is the the kwarg parameter and it is the key path name of which the value should be fetched
            :type pstr_keypath: String
            :param pstr_keypath_type: pstr_keypath_type the kwarg parameter and it is the  key path type i.e.absolute or relative
            :type pstr_keypath_type: String
            :param pstr_key_input: pstr_key_input  is the the kwarg parameter and it is key value  which is presented in key path
            :type pstr_key_input: String
            :param pstr_expected_message: pstr_expected_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the expected value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_expected_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message: pstr_actual_message  is the the kwarg parameter and it is the actual value of a this and this will be inserted in kibana
            :type pstr_actual_message: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_pass: pstr_actual_message_on_pass kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is True
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_pass: String
            :param pstr_actual_message_on_fail: pstr_actual_message_on_fail kwarg parameter is the actual message that would insert into kibana when a validation is False
            :type pstr_actual_message_on_fail: String
            :param pobj_api_response: API Response Object
            :type pobj_api_response: Response

            :return: Boolean
            Examples:
                |  assert_response_contains("Value","Json",json=Json_data,pstr_key="key name",pbool_nested=True,pstr_actual_message_on_pass="Response contains given value",pstr_actual_message_on_fail="Response doesn't contain given value")

            .. warning::
                |  if "pstr_actual_message_on_pass" passed pstr_actual_message_on_fail should also be passed and they should not be equal
            """
            try:
                assert self.verify_response_contains(
                    pstr_value, pstr_response_type, pbool_insert_kibana=True, **kwargs
                )
            except AssertionError as ae:
                assertion_err_msg = "Assertion Failed at step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(assertion_err_msg)
                pytest.fail(assertion_err_msg, pytrace=False)
            except Exception as e:
                err_msg = "Exception occured during assertion validation in the step --> " + str(
                    pytest.globalDict["step_name"]
                )
                self.logger.exception(err_msg)
                pytest.fail(err_msg, pytrace=False)
